        <script type="text/javascript">
         jQuery(document).ready(function($){update_left_radios();setInterval(function(){update_left_radios();},60000);function update_left_radios(){return false;var days=["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday","Sunday"];var radio_ids='959,938,1082,956,1058,1068,602,825,1006';var browserDate=new Date(),diffWithArgentina=((browserDate.getTimezoneOffset()/60-3)*3600000),date=new Date(browserDate.getTime()+diffWithArgentina);var today=days[date.getDay()];var hour=date.getHours()+':'+date.getMinutes();$.ajax({url:'https://reproductor.cienradios.com.ar/player/apiV2/GetProgramasActualesDeRadios?idsRadios='+radio_ids+'&cantidadProgramas=4',success:function(response){$.each(response,function(k,v){var emisora_id=v.emisora.id;var showed_program_name=$('.menu-radios-info[data-id="'+emisora_id+'"]').find(".menu-radios-programing-title.first").html();if(v.programas[0].nombre!=showed_program_name){console.log('Actualizando programas en vivo en menu...');var items=$('.menu-radios-info[data-id="'+emisora_id+'"] .menu-radios-programing-item');$.each(items,function(k,item){$(item).find('.menu-radios-programing-title').html(v.programas[k].nombre);$(item).find('.menu-radios-programing-host').html(v.programas[k].descripcion);if(k>0)$(item).find('.time').html(v.programas[k].horarioInicio);});$('.radios-vivo-item[data-id="'+emisora_id+'"] .radios-vivo-item-subtitle').html(v.programas[0].nombre);}else{}});}});}});
        </script>
